RACE OVERVIEW
=============
The 2024 British Grand Prix at Silverstone was a memorable race affected by intermittent rain, leading to strategic challenges for the teams. Lewis Hamilton emerged victorious, claiming a record-breaking ninth win at the Silverstone circuit. Max Verstappen finished second after a late-race charge, and Lando Norris secured third place. The race saw George Russell initially leading from pole position, but he struggled with pace as the rain intensified. Sergio Perez had a difficult race, finishing outside the points. The changeable conditions and strategic decisions made for an exciting and unpredictable race.
